# Domain Lineage: Kafka Producer Config Propagation Path

## Your Task

Trace how the `acks` producer configuration value propagates through the Kafka codebase. Find all Java source files in `apache/kafka` that: 1. Define the `acks` configuration constant (in `ProducerConfig`). 2. Read and validate the `acks` value during producer initialization. 3. Encode the `acks` value into the produce request protocol (the `ProduceRequest` builder). 4. Apply the `acks` value in the broker-side partition leader to determine write acknowledgment behavior. Report the repo, file path, class name, and the role in the propagation chain for each file.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Perfect! I've successfully traced the complete propagation path of the `acks` producer configuration through the Kafka codebase. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Propagation Chain Summary

The `acks` value propagates through **8 key files**:

1. **ProducerConfig.java** - Defines `ACKS_CONFIG` constant and validates values (0, 1, -1/"all")
2. **KafkaProducer.java** - Reads and parses the acks value during producer initialization
3. **Sender.java** - Stores acks and uses it to build ProduceRequest objects
4. **ProduceRequest.json** - Protocol schema definition for the Acks field
5. **ProduceRequest.java** - Protocol class that carries the acks value in the request
6. **KafkaApis.scala** - Broker-side handler that checks acks for throttling and response decisions
7. **ReplicaManager.scala** - Validates acks and determines if delayed produce operations are needed
8. **Partition.scala** - Partition leader that enforces min ISR when acks == -1
9. **DelayedProduce.scala** - Monitors replication progress based on the required acks level

## Key Control Points

- **acks=0**: Fire-and-forget (no response sent, request throttling exempted)
- **acks=1**: Leader acknowledgment only
- **acks=-1** ("all"): All in-sync replicas must acknowledge (enforces min ISR, uses delayed produce operations)

The answer file at `/workspace/answer.json` contains comprehensive details including all relevant files, symbols, and a detailed narrative of the propagation chain.

This controls the \\\"\\n125:                                            + \\\" durability of records that are sent. The following settings are allowed: \\\"\\n126:                                            + \\\" <ul>\\\"\\n127:                                            + \\\" <li><code>acks=0</code> If set to zero then the producer will not wait for any acknowledgment from the\\\"\\n128:                                            + \\\" server at all. The record will be immediately added to the socket buffer and considered sent. No guarantee can be\\\"\\n129:                                            + \\\" made that the server has received the record in this case, and the <code>retries</code> configuration will not\\\"\\n130:                                            + \\\" take effect (as the client won't generally know of any failures). The offset given back for each record will\\\"\\n131:                                            + \\\" always be set to <code>-1</code>.\\\"\\n132:                                            + \\\" <li><code>acks=1</code> This will mean the leader will write the record to its local log but will respond\\\"\\n133:                                            + \\\" without awaiting full acknowledgement from all followers. In this case should the leader fail immediately after\\\"\\n134:                                            + \\\" acknowledging the record but before the followers have replicated it then the record will be lost.\\\"\\n135:                                            + \\\" <li><code>acks=all</code> This means the leader will wait for the full set of in-sync replicas to\\\"\\n136:                                            + \\\" acknowledge the record. This guarantees that the record will not be lost as long as at least one in-sync replica\\\"\\n137:                                            + \\\" remains alive.
